        }

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

        <p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

Note the issue was originally reported in 



<span class="line"><!---->Note the issue was originally reported in <!----></span>





https://crbug.com/1416794#c8



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://crbug.com/1416794#c8"><!---->https://crbug.com/1416794#c8<!----></a>





, but as the issue was closed as WontFix, I'm resubmitting the issue in case it gets missed. This report reports two vulnerabilties:



<span class="line"><!---->, but as the issue was closed as WontFix, I'm resubmitting the issue in case it gets missed. This report reports two vulnerabilties:<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





1. Download Protection Service does not shorten URL in referrer chains



<span class="line"><!---->1. Download Protection Service does not shorten URL in referrer chains<!----></span>



<br>





2. Even if the danger type was DOWNLOAD_DANGER_TYPE_MAYBE_DANGEROUS_CONTENT, if Safe Browsing check fails, no warning is shown to the user



<span class="line"><!---->2. Even if the danger type was DOWNLOAD_DANGER_TYPE_MAYBE_DANGEROUS_CONTENT, if Safe Browsing check fails, no warning is shown to the user<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





VULNERABILITY DETAILS



<b class="line"><!---->VULNERABILITY DETAILS<!----></b>



<br>





1. Safe Browsing (



<span class="line"><!---->1. Safe Browsing (<!----></span>





https://sb-ssl.google.com/safebrowsing/clientreport/download



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://sb-ssl.google.com/safebrowsing/clientreport/download"><!---->https://sb-ssl.google.com/safebrowsing/clientreport/download<!----></a>





)



<span class="line"><!---->)<!----></span>





 fails with 413 (Payload Too Large), if the body exceed about 20MB.



<span class="line"><!----> fails with 413 (Payload Too Large), if the body exceed about 20MB.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





AddEventUrlToReferrerChain[1] does not shorten data URIs in the URL and server redirect chain, so the download check can be bypassed if the data URI exceeds ~8MB.



<span class="line"><!---->AddEventUrlToReferrerChain[1] does not shorten data URIs in the URL and server redirect chain, so the download check can be bypassed if the data URI exceeds ~8MB.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





PPAPIDownloadRequest[2] may also be vulnerable, but I'm not sure whether the requestor origin can be a data URI.



<span class="line"><!---->PPAPIDownloadRequest[2] may also be vulnerable, but I'm not sure whether the requestor origin can be a data URI.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





As mentioned in the original issue, this is actively exploited in the wild, not sure intended or not, as downloader trojans use data URIs to bypass the domain check.



<span class="line"><!---->As mentioned in the original issue, this is actively exploited in the wild, not sure intended or not, as downloader trojans use data URIs to bypass the domain check.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Please find attached the suggested patch.



<span class="line"><!---->Please find attached the suggested patch.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





2. Even if the danger type was DOWNLOAD_DANGER_TYPE_MAYBE_DANGEROUS_CONTENT, if Safe Browsing check is not perfomed or failed, the DownloadCheckResult is set to UNKNOWN[3] and the danger type is reset to DOWNLOAD_DANGER_TYPE_NOT_DANGEROUS[4]. As a result, no warning is shown to the user, and this may give the user a false sense of security and inconsistent experience.



<span class="line"><!---->2. Even if the danger type was DOWNLOAD_DANGER_TYPE_MAYBE_DANGEROUS_CONTENT, if Safe Browsing check is not perfomed or failed, the DownloadCheckResult is set to UNKNOWN[3] and the danger type is reset to DOWNLOAD_DANGER_TYPE_NOT_DANGEROUS[4]. As a result, no warning is shown to the user, and this may give the user a false sense of security and inconsistent experience.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





If the result is unknown for any other reasons Safe Browsing actually reporting unknown, the download should be treated as dangerous as if the Safe Browsing is disabled[5] or at least uncommon.



<span class="line"><!---->If the result is unknown for any other reasons Safe Browsing actually reporting unknown, the download should be treated as dangerous as if the Safe Browsing is disabled[5] or at least uncommon.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

VERSION



<b class="line"><!---->VERSION<!----></b>



<br>





Chrome Version: 110.0.5481.100 stable



<span class="line"><!---->Chrome Version: 110.0.5481.100 stable<!----></span>



<br>





Operating System: Windows 11 21H2



<span class="line"><!---->Operating System: Windows 11 21H2<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





REPRODUCTION CASE



<b class="line"><!---->REPRODUCTION CASE<!----></b>



<br>





1. Enable Safe Browsing in chrome://settings/security.



<span class="line"><!---->1. Enable Safe Browsing in chrome://settings/security.<!----></span>



<br>





2. Open chrome://safe-browsing/#tab-download-protection.



<span class="line"><!---->2. Open chrome://safe-browsing/#tab-download-protection.<!----></span>



<br>





3. Serve the attached poc.html over HTTP and navigate to the page.



<span class="line"><!---->3. Serve the attached poc.html over HTTP and navigate to the page.<!----></span>



<br>





4. Click "7MB" and check the Download response (ClientDownloadResponse) is received.



<span class="line"><!---->4. Click "7MB" and check the Download response (ClientDownloadResponse) is received.<!----></span>



<br>





5. Click "8MB" and check the Download response (ClientDownloadResponse) is not received.



<span class="line"><!---->5. Click "8MB" and check the Download response (ClientDownloadResponse) is not received.<!----></span>



<br>





6. Check the warning, e.g., "This type of file can harm your computer", is not shown.



<span class="line"><!---->6. Check the warning, e.g., "This type of file can harm your computer", is not shown.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

Thanks for the report! I'm able to reproduce the 8 MB version having a ClientDownloadResponse while the 7 MB version does not. I can also see that the SBClientDownload.CheckDownloadStats histogram has a value of 10 for the 7 MB one ("safe") while the 8 MB version has a value of 5 ("server ping failed"). I think we should be able to simulate what happens for an unsafe download (rather than a safe one) with a local build, temporarily modifying the verdict to unsafe. 



<span class="line"><!---->Thanks for the report! I'm able to reproduce the 8 MB version having a ClientDownloadResponse while the 7 MB version does not. I can also see that the SBClientDownload.CheckDownloadStats histogram has a value of 10 for the 7 MB one ("safe") while the 8 MB version has a value of 5 ("server ping failed"). I think we should be able to simulate what happens for an unsafe download (rather than a safe one) with a local build, temporarily modifying the verdict to unsafe. <!----></span>



<br>



<br>





drubery@: Could you PTAL to see if this is able to bypass the ping for unsafe downloads?



<span class="line"><!---->drubery@: Could you PTAL to see if this is able to bypass the ping for unsafe downloads?<!----></span>

          <a class="comment-link" href="?id=1417325#c8">Comment 8<!----></a>

          
        by

There seem to be more ways to make the request larger than 20 MB. Please let me know if they need separate issues to be filed.



<span class="line"><!---->There seem to be more ways to make the request larger than 20 MB. Please let me know if they need separate issues to be filed.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





3. BinaryFeatureExtractor does not truncate debug data over 20 MB.



<span class="line"><!---->3. BinaryFeatureExtractor does not truncate debug data over 20 MB.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





VULNERABILITY DETAILS



<span class="line"><!---->VULNERABILITY DETAILS<!----></span>



<br>





3. BinaryFeatureExtractor attaches the whole debug data (IMAGE_DEBUG_DIRECTORY) in ClientDownloadRequest[1], but does not truncate even if it exceeds 20 MB.



<span class="line"><!---->3. BinaryFeatureExtractor attaches the whole debug data (IMAGE_DEBUG_DIRECTORY) in ClientDownloadRequest[1], but does not truncate even if it exceeds 20 MB.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Since the debugging information does not affect the execution, the attacker can easily pad IMAGE_DEBUG_DIRECTORY with dummy data and bypass safe browsing check.



<span class="line"><!---->Since the debugging information does not affect the execution, the attacker can easily pad IMAGE_DEBUG_DIRECTORY with dummy data and bypass safe browsing check.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





[1] 



<span class="line"><!---->[1] <!----></span>





https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:chrome/common/safe_browsing/binary_feature_extractor_win.cc;l=166;drc=856552dde046dcfc782793484b5f4af4743552a1



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:chrome/common/safe_browsing/binary_feature_extractor_win.cc;l=166;drc=856552dde046dcfc782793484b5f4af4743552a1"><!---->https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:chrome/common/safe_browsing/binary_feature_extractor_win.cc;l=166;drc=856552dde046dcfc782793484b5f4af4743552a1<!----></a>



<br>



<br>





REPRODUCTION CASE



<span class="line"><!---->REPRODUCTION CASE<!----></span>



<br>





1. Enable Safe Browsing in chrome://settings/security.



<span class="line"><!---->1. Enable Safe Browsing in chrome://settings/security.<!----></span>



<br>





2. Open chrome://safe-browsing/#tab-download-protection.



<span class="line"><!---->2. Open chrome://safe-browsing/#tab-download-protection.<!----></span>



<br>





3. Download big-debug.exe (included in big-debug.zip or assembled via `nasm -f bin -o big-debug.exe big-debug.asm`) over HTTP.



<span class="line"><!---->3. Download big-debug.exe (included in big-debug.zip or assembled via `nasm -f bin -o big-debug.exe big-debug.asm`) over HTTP.<!----></span>



<br>





4. Check the Download response (ClientDownloadResponse) is not received.



<span class="line"><!---->4. Check the Download response (ClientDownloadResponse) is not received.<!----></span>



<br>





5. Check the warning, e.g., "This type of file can harm your computer", is not shown.



<span class="line"><!---->5. Check the warning, e.g., "This type of file can harm your computer", is not shown.<!----></span>

*** Boilerplate reminders! ***



<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.

        .chops-autocomplete-container {
          position: relative;
        }

          padding: 0;

          color: var(--chops-link-color);
          position: absolute;
          background: var(--chops-white);
          border: var(--chops-accessible-border);
          z-index: 999;
          box-shadow: 2px 3px 8px 0px hsla(0, 0%, 0%, 0.3);
          border-spacing: 0;
          border-collapse: collapse;
          /* In the case when the autocomplete extends the
           * height of the viewport, we want to make sure
           * there's spacing. */

          display: block;
          min-width: 100px;
          max-height: 500px;
          overflow: auto;

          cursor: pointer;
          transition: background 0.2s ease-in-out;
